            <!-- Fighting the Space Between Inline Block Elements

            <div class="views-row views-row-1 views-row-odd views-row-first">
             <article about="/artikkeli/vanhemmuus/synnytys-ei-tee-naisesta-oraakkelia-mieti-missa-heilutat-aitikorttia" class="node-3195888 node node-article node-promoted view-mode-medium_teaser node-medium_teaser node-article-medium_teaser tagged-kolumnit tagged-vanhemmuus tagged-äitiys tagged-kasvatus tagged-jaksaminen tagged-marjut-ollila has-main-media clearfix" typeof="sioc:Item foaf:Document">
              <a href="/artikkeli/vanhemmuus/synnytys-ei-tee-naisesta-oraakkelia-mieti-missa-heilutat-aitikorttia">
               <div class="media">
                <div class="field field-name-field-main-media field-type-file field-label-hidden">

          <h2 class="pane-title">
           <a href="/node/2401179">
            Videot
           </a>

         <div class="pane-content">
          <div class="view view-themes view-id-themes view-display-id-most_recent_pane slider-six-cols view-dom-id-30b967591d85ec4e8d36b032ce156e3a">
           <div class="view-content">
            <!-- Fighting the Space Between Inline Block Elements
